This covenant was differently administered in the time of the law, and in the time of the gospel:<sup>i</sup> under the law, it was administered by promises, prophecies, sacrifices, circumcision, the paschal lamb, and other types and ordinances delivered to the people of the Jews, all fore-signifying Christ to come:<sup>k</sup> which were, for that time, sufficient and efficacious, through the operation of the Spirit, to instruct and build up the elect in faith in the promised Messiah,<sup>l</sup> by whom they had full remission of sins, and eternal salvation; and is called, the Old Testament.<sup>m</sup></p><p><sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_3.6-9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 3:6-9</a>. <sup>k</sup>Heb 8-10; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:11-12</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_5.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 5:7</a>. <sup>l</sup>Cor 10:1-4; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_11.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 11:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_8.56" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 8:56</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.7-9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 3:7-9</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>.</p><p>6. Under the gospel, when Christ, the substance,<sup>n</sup> was exhibited, the ordinances in which this covenant is dispensed are the preaching of the Word, and the administration of the sacraments of Baptism and the Lord’s Supper:<sup>o</sup> which, though fewer in number, and administered with more simplicity, and less outward glory; yet, in them, it is held forth in more fulness, evidence, and spiritual efficacy,<sup>p</sup> to all nations, both Jews and Gentiles;<sup>q</sup> and is called the New Testament.<sup>r</sup> There are not therefore two covenants of grace, differing in substance, but one and the same, under various dispensations.<sup>s</sup></p><p><sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:17</a>. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19-20</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.23-25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:23-25</a>. <sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_12.22-28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 12:22-28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Jer_31.33-34" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jer 31:33-34</a>. <sup>q</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.15-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:15-19</a>. <sup>r</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_22.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 22:20</a>. <sup>s</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 3:14</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.21-23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 3:21-23</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">30</a>. <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_32.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 32:1</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:3</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">6</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.16-17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">16-17</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.23-24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">23-24</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_13.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 13:8</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_15.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 15:11</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp8"></a></p><h2>&nbsp;Chapter 8 –&nbsp;Of Christ the Mediator</h2><p>1. It pleased God, in His eternal purpose, to choose and ordain the Lord Jesus, His only begotten Son, to be the Mediator between God and man;<sup>a</sup> the Prophet,<sup>b</sup> Priest,<sup>c</sup> and King,<sup>d</sup> the Head and Saviour of His Church,<sup>e</sup> the Heir of all things,<sup>f</sup> and Judge of the world:<sup>g</sup> unto whom He did from all eternity give a people, to be His seed,<sup>h</sup> and to be by Him in time redeemed, called, justified, sanctified, and glorified.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_42.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 42:1</a>; 1&nbsp;Pet&nbsp;1:19-20; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_3.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John&nbsp;3:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_2.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 2:5</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_3.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 3:22</a>.&nbsp;<sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_5.5-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 5:5-6</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_2.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps&nbsp;2:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_1.33" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 1:33</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_5.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 5:23</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_1.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 1:2</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_17.31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 17:31</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_17.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 17:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_22.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 22:30</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_53.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 53:10</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_2.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 2:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_55.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 55:4-5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_1.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 1:30</a>.</p><p>2. The Son of God, the second person in the Trinity, being very and eternal God, of one substance and equal with the Father, did, when the fulness of time was come, take upon Him man’s nature,<sup>k</sup> with all the essential properties and common infirmities thereof, yet without sin:<sup>l</sup> being conceived by the power of the Holy Ghost, in the womb of the virgin Mary, of her substance.<sup>m</sup> So that two whole, perfect, and distinct natures, the Godhead and the manhood, were inseparably joined together in one person, without conversion, composition, or confusion.<sup>n</sup> Which person is very God, and very man, yet one Christ, the only Mediator between God and man.<sup>o</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_1.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John&nbsp;1:1</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_1.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>; 1&nbsp;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_5.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 5:20</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Phil_2.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Phil 2:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_4.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 4:4</a>. <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_2.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 2:14</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_2.16-17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">16-17</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_4.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 4:15</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_1.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke&nbsp;1:27</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_1.31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">31</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_1.35" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">35</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_4.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 4:4</a>. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_1.35" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 1:35</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_9.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 9:5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Peter_3.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Peter 3:18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_3.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 3:16</a>. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_1.3-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 1:3-4</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_1.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_2.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 2:5</a>.</p><p>3. The Lord Jesus, in His human nature thus united to the divine, was sanctified and anointed with the Holy Spirit, above measure,<sup>p</sup> having in Him all the treasures of wisdom and knowledge;<sup>q</sup> in whom it pleased the Father that all fulness should dwell;<sup>r</sup> to the end that, being holy, harmless, undefiled, and full of grace and truth,<sup>s</sup> He might be thoroughly furnished to&nbsp;execute the office of a mediator&nbsp;and surety.<sup>t</sup> Which&nbsp;office He took not unto Himself, but was thereunto called by His Father,<sup>u</sup> who put all power and judgment into His hand, and gave Him commandment to execute the same.<sup>w</sup></p><p><sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_45.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 45:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_3.34" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 3:34</a>. <sup>q</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:3</a>. <sup>r</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_1.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 1:19</a>. <sup>s</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_7.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 7:26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_1.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 1:14</a>. <sup>t</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.38" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 10:38</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_12.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 12:24</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_7.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 7:22</a>. <sup>u</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_5.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 5:4-5</a>. <sup>w</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_5.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 5:22</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_5.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">27</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.36" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:36</a>.</p><p>4. This office the Lord Jesus did most willingly undertake;<sup>x</sup> which that He might discharge, He was made under the law,<sup>y</sup> and did perfectly fulfil it,<sup>z</sup> endured most grievous torments immediately in His soul,<sup>a</sup> and most painful sufferings in His body;<sup>b</sup> was crucified, and died;<sup>c</sup> was buried, and remained under the power of death; yet saw no corruption.<sup>d</sup> On the third day He arose from the dead,<sup>e</sup> with the same body in which He suffered,<sup>f</sup> with which also he ascended into heaven, and there sitteth at the right hand of His Father,<sup>g</sup> making intercession,<sup>h</sup> and shall return to judge men and angels at the end of the world.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>x</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_40.7-8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 40:7-8</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.5-10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 10:5-10</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_10.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 10:18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Phil_2.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Phil 2:8</a>. <sup>y</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_4.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 4:4</a>. <sup>z</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_3.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 3:15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_5.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 5:17</a>. <sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_26.37-38" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 26:37-38</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_22.44" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 22:44</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_27.46" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 27:46</a>. <sup>b</sup>Matt 26-27. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Phil_2.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Phil 2:8</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.23-24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:23-24</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">27</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_13.37" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 13:37</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:9</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_15.3-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 15:3-4</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_20.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 20:25</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_20.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">27</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_16.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 16:19</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.34" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:34</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 9:24</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_7.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 7:25</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_14.9-10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 14:9-10</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_1.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 1:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.42" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 10:42</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_13.40-42" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 13:40-42</a>; Jude 6; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Pet_2.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Pet 2:4</a>.</p><p>5. The Lord Jesus, by His perfect obedience, and sacrifice of Himself, which He, through the eternal Spirit, once offered up unto God, hath fully satisfied the justice of His Father;<sup>k</sup> and purchased, not only reconciliation, but an everlasting inheritance in the kingdom of heaven, for all those whom the Father hath given unto Him.<sup>l</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_5.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 5:19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 9:14</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 10:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_5.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 5:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.25-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 3:25-26</a>. <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Dan_9.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Dan 9:24</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Dan_9.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_1.19-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 1:19-20</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:11</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_17.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 17:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 9:12</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">15</a>.</p><p>6. Although the work of redemption was not actually wrought by Christ till after His incarnation, yet the virtue, efficacy, and benefits thereof were communicated unto the elect in all ages successively from the beginning of the world, in and by those promises, types, and sacrifices, wherein He was revealed, and signified to be the seed of the woman which should bruise the serpent’s head; and the Lamb slain from the beginning of the world: being yesterday and today the same, and for ever.<sup>m</sup></p><p><sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_4.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 4:4-5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_3.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 3:15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_13.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rev 13:8</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_13.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 13:8</a>.</p><p>7. Christ, in the work of mediation, acteth according to both natures, by each nature doing that which is proper to itself:<sup>n</sup> yet, by reason of the unity of the person, that which is proper to one nature, is sometimes in Scripture attributed to the person denominated by the other nature.<sup>o</sup></p><p><sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 9:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_3.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 3:18</a>. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_20.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 20:28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_3.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 3:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_3.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 3:16</a>.</p><p>8. To all those for whom Christ hath purchased redemption, He doth certainly and effectually apply and communicate the same,<sup>p</sup> making intercession for them,<sup>q</sup> and revealing unto them, in and by the Word, the mysteries of salvation,<sup>r</sup> effectually persuading them by His Spirit to believe and obey, and governing their hearts by His Word and Spirit,<sup>s</sup> overcoming all their enemies by His almighty power and wisdom, in such manner, and ways, as are most consonant to His wonderful and unsearchable dispensation.<sup>t</sup></p><p><sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_6.37" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John&nbsp;6:37</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_6.39" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">39</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_10.15-16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 10:15-16</a>. <sup>q</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_2.1-2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John&nbsp;2:1-2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.34" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom&nbsp;8:34</a>. <sup>r</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_15.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John&nbsp;15:13</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_15.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.7-9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph&nbsp;1:7-9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_17.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John&nbsp;17:6</a>. <sup>s</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_14.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 14:26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_12.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 12:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_4.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 4:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:9</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_15.18-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 15:18-19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_17.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 17:17</a>. <sup>t</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_110.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 110:1</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_15.25-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 15:25-26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mal_4.2-3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mal 4:2-3</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:15</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp9"></a></p><h2>Chapter 9 – Of Free Will</h2><p>1. God hath endued the will of man with that natural liberty, that it is neither forced, nor by any absolute necessity of nature determined to good or evil.<sup>a</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_17.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 17:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=James_1.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">James 1:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_30.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 30:19</a>.</p><p>2. Man, in his state of innocency, had freedom and power to will and to do that which was good, and well pleasing to God;<sup>b</sup> but yet mutably, so that he might fall from it.<sup>c</sup></p><p><sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eccl_7.29" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eccl 7:29</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_1.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 1:26</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_2.16-17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 2:16-17</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_3.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 3:6</a>.</p><p>3. Man, by his fall into a state of sin, hath wholly lost all ability of will to any spiritual good accompanying salvation:<sup>d</sup> so as, a natural man, being altogether averse from that good,<sup>e</sup> and dead in sin,<sup>f</sup> is not able, by his own strength, to convert himself, or to prepare himself thereunto.<sup>g</sup></p><p><sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_5.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 5:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom8:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_15.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 15:5</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 3:10</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">12</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:1</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:13</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_6.44" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 6:44</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_6.65" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">65</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.2-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:2-5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_2.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 2:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.3-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tit 3:3-5</a>.</p><p>4. When God converts a sinner, and translates him into the state of grace, He freeth him from his natural bondage under sin;<sup>h</sup> and, by His grace alone, enables him freely to will and to do that which is spiritually good;<sup>i</sup> yet so, as that by reason of his remaining corruption, he doth not perfectly, nor only, will that which is good, but doth also will that which is evil.<sup>k</sup></p><p><sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_1.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 1:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_8.34" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 8:34</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_8.36" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">36</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Phil_2.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Phil 2:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:18</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">22</a>. <sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_5.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 5:17</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_7.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 7:15</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_7.18-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">18-19</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_7.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_7.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">21</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_7.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">23</a>.</p><p>5. The will of man is made perfectly and immutably free to good alone, in the state of glory only.<sup>l</sup></p><p><sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_4.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 4:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_12.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 12:23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_3.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 3:2</a>; Jude 24.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp10"></a></p><h2>Chapter 10 –&nbsp;Of Effectual Calling</h2><p>1. All those whom God hath predestinated unto life, and those only, He is pleased in His appointed and accepted time effectually to call,<sup>a</sup> by His Word and Spirit,<sup>b</sup> out of that state of sin and death, in which they are by nature, to grace and salvation by Jesus Christ;<sup>c</sup> enlightening their minds spiritually and savingly to understand the things of God;<sup>d</sup> taking away their heart of stone, and giving unto them a heart of flesh;<sup>e</sup> renewing their wills, and by His almighty power determining them to that which is good,<sup>f</sup> and effectually drawing them to Jesus Christ:<sup>g</sup> yet so, as they come most freely, being made willing by His grace.<sup>h</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:30</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_11.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 11:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.10-11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:10-11</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Thess_2.13-14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Thess 2:13-14</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Thess_2.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_3.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 3:3</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_3.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">6</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.1-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:1-5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Tim_1.9-10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Tim 1:9-10</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_26.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 26:18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_2.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 2:10</a>, <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_2.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.17-18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:17-18</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_36.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 36:26</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_11.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 11:19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Phil_2.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Phil 2:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_30.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 30:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_36.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 36:27</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_6.44-45" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 6:44-45</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Song_1.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Song 1:4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_110.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 110:3</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_6.37" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 6:37</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.16-18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:16-18</a>.</p><p>2. This effectual call is of God’s free and special grace alone, not from anything at all foreseen in man,<sup>i</sup> who is altogether passive therein, until being quickened and renewed by the Holy Spirit,<sup>k</sup> he is thereby enabled to answer this call, and to embrace the grace offered and conveyed in it.<sup>l</sup></p><p><sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Tim_1.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Tim 1:9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tit 3:4-5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:4-5</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.8-9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">8-9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_9.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 9:11</a>. <sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_2.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 2:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:5</a>. <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_6.37" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 6:37</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_36.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 36:27</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_5.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 5:25</a>.</p><p>3. Elect infants, dying in infancy, are regenerated, and saved by Christ through the Spirit,<sup>m</sup> who worketh when, and where, and how He pleaseth:<sup>n</sup> so also, are all other elect persons who are uncapable of being outwardly called by the ministry of the Word.<sup>o</sup></p><p><sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_18.15-16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 18:15-16</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.38-39" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:38-39</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_3.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 3:3</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_3.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">5</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_5.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 5:12</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:9</a> [compared together]. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_3.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 3:8</a>. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_5.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 5:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_4.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 4:12</a>.</p><p>4. Others, not elected, although they may be called by the ministry of the Word,<sup>p</sup> and may have some common operations of the Spirit,<sup>q</sup> yet they never truly come unto Christ, and therefore cannot be saved:<sup>r</sup> much less can men, not professing the Christian religion, be saved in any other way whatsoever, be they never so diligent to frame their lives according to the light of nature, and the law of that religion they do profess.<sup>s</sup> And, to assert and maintain that they may, is very pernicious, and to be detested.<sup>t</sup></p><p><sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_22.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 22:14</a>. <sup>q</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_7.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 7:22</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_13.20-21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 13:20-21</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_6.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 6:4-5</a>. <sup>r</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_6.64-66" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 6:64-66</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_8.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 8:24</a>. <sup>s</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_4.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 4:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_14.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 14:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_4.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 4:22</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_17.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 17:3</a>. <sup>t</sup>2 John 9-11; 1 Cor 16:22; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_1.6-8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 1:6-8</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp11"></a></p><h2>Chapter 11 –&nbsp;Of Justification</h2><p>1. Those whom God effectually calleth, He also freely justifieth:<sup>a</sup> not by infusing righteousness into them, but by pardoning their sins, and by accounting and accepting their persons as righteous, not for anything wrought in them, or done by them, but for Christ’s sake alone; nor by imputing faith itself, the act of believing, or any other evangelical obedience to them, as their righteousness, but by imputing the obedience and satisfaction of Christ unto them,<sup>b</sup> they receiving and resting on Him and His righteousness by faith; which faith they have not of themselves, it is the gift of God.<sup>c</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:30</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 3:24</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.5-8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:5-8</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_5.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 5:19</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_5.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">21</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 3:22</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.24-25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">24-25</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.27-28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">27-28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tit 3:5</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Jer_23.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jer 23:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_1.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 1:30</a>, <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_1.31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">31</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_5.17-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 5:17-19</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.43" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 10:43</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_2.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 2:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Phil_3.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Phil 3:9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_13.38-39" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 13:38-39</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.7-8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:7-8</a>.</p><p>2. Faith, thus receiving and resting on Christ and His righteousness, is the alone instrument of justification;<sup>d</sup> yet it is not alone in the person justified, but is ever accompanied with all other saving graces, and is no dead faith, but worketh by love.<sup>e</sup></p><p><sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_1.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 1:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 3:28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_5.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 5:1</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=James_2.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">James 2:17</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=James_2.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">22</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=James_2.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_5.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 5:6</a>.</p><p>3. Christ, by His obedience and death, did fully discharge the debt of all those that are thus justified, and did make a proper, real, and full satisfaction to His Father’s justice in their behalf.<sup>f</sup> Yet, inasmuch as He was given by the Father for them;<sup>g</sup> and His obedience and satisfaction accepted in their stead;<sup>h</sup> &nbsp;and both freely, not for anything in them; their justification is only of free grace;<sup>i</sup> that both the exact justice, and rich grace of God, might be glorified in the justification of sinners.<sup>k</sup></p><p><sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_5.8-10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 5:8-10</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_5.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_5.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_2.5-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 2:5-6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 10:10</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Dan_9.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Dan 9:24</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Dan_9.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_53.4-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 53:4-6</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_53.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_53.10-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">10-12</a>.&nbsp;<sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:32</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_5.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 5:21</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_3.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 3:17</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_5.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 5:2</a>; <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 3:24</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:7</a>; <sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 3:26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:7</a>.</p><p>4. God did, from all eternity, decree to justify all the elect,<sup>l</sup> and Christ did, in the fulness of time, die for their sins, and rise again for their justification:<sup>m</sup> nevertheless, they are not justified, until the Holy Spirit doth, in due time, actually apply Christ unto them.<sup>n</sup></p><p><sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 3:8</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_1.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 1:2</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_1.19-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">19-20</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:30</a>.&nbsp;<sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_4.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal&nbsp;4:4</a>;&nbsp;1&nbsp;Tim&nbsp;2:6; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:25</a>. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_1.21-22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 1:21-22</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_2.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 2:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.3-7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tit 3:3-7</a>.</p><p>5. God doth continue to forgive the sins of those that are justified:<sup>o</sup> and, although they can never fall from the state of justification;<sup>p</sup> yet they may, by their sins, fall under God’s fatherly displeasure, and not have the light of His countenance restored unto them, until they humble themselves, confess their sins, beg pardon, and renew their faith and repentance.<sup>q</sup></p><p><sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_6.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 6:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_1.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 1:7</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_1.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_2.1-2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 2:1-2</a>. <sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_22.32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 22:32</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_10.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 10:28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 10:14</a>. <sup>q</sup> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_89.31-33" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 89:31-33</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_51.7-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 51:7-12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_32.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 32:5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_26.75" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 26:75</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:30</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">32</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_1.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 1:20</a>.</p><p>6. The justification of believers under the Old Testament was, in all these respects, one and the same with the justification of believers under the New Testament.<sup>r</sup></p><p><sup>r</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 3:9</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.13-14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">13-14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.22-24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:22-24</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_13.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 13:8</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp12"></a></p><h2>Chapter 12 –&nbsp;Of Adoption</h2><p>1. All those that are justified, God vouchsafeth, in and for His only Son Jesus Christ, to make partakers of the grace of adoption:<sup>a</sup> by which they are taken into the number, and enjoy the liberties and privileges of the children of God,<sup>b</sup> have His name put upon them,<sup>c</sup> receive the spirit of adoption,<sup>d</sup> have access to the throne of grace with boldness,<sup>e</sup> are enabled to cry, Abba, Father,<sup>f</sup> are pitied,<sup>g</sup> protected,<sup>h</sup> provided for,<sup>i</sup> and chastened by Him as by a Father;<sup>k</sup> yet never cast off,<sup>l</sup> but sealed to the day of redemption,<sup>m</sup> and inherit the promises,<sup>n</sup> as heirs of everlasting salvation.<sup>o</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:5</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_4.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 4:4-5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:17</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_1.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 1:12</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Jer_14.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jer 14:9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_6.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 6:18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_3.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rev 3:12</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:15</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_3.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 3:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_5.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 5:2</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_4.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 4:6</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_103.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 103:13</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Prov_14.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Prov 14:26</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_6.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 6:30</a>, <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_6.32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">32</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_5.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 5:7</a>. <sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_12.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 12:6</a>. <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Lam_3.31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Lam 3:31</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_4.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 4:30</a>. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_6.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 6:12</a>. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_1.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 1:3</a>, <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_1.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_1.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 1:14</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp13"></a></p><h2>Chapter 13 –&nbsp;Of Sanctification</h2><p>1. They who are effectually called and regenerated, having a new heart and a new spirit created in them, are further sanctified, really and personally, through the virtue of Christ’s death&nbsp;and resurrection,<sup>a</sup> by His Word and Spirit dwelling in them:<sup>b</sup> the dominion of the whole body of sin is destroyed,<sup>c</sup> and the several lusts thereof are more and more weakened and mortified;<sup>d</sup> and they more and more quickened and strengthened in all saving graces,<sup>e</sup> to the practice of true holiness, without which no man shall see the Lord.<sup>f</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_6.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 6:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_20.32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 20:32</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Phil_3.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Phil 3:10</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.5-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:5-6</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_17.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 17:17</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_5.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 5:26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Thess_2.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Thess 2:13</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:6</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_5.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 5:24</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:13</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_1.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 1:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_3.16-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 3:16-19</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_7.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 7:1</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_12.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 12:14</a>.</p><p>2. This sanctification is throughout, in the whole man;<sup>g</sup> yet imperfect in this life, there abiding still some remnants of corruption in every part:<sup>h</sup> whence ariseth a continual and irreconcilable war; the flesh lusting against the Spirit, and the Spirit against the flesh.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Thess_5.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Thess 5:23</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_1.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 1:10</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_7.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 7:18</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_7.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Phil_3.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Phil 3:12</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_5.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 5:17</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_2.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 2:11</a>.</p><p>3. In which war, although the remaining corruption, for a time, may much prevail;<sup>k</sup> yet through the continual supply of strength from the sanctifying Spirit of Christ, the regenerate part doth overcome;<sup>l</sup> and so, the saints grow in grace,<sup>m</sup> perfecting holiness in the fear of God.<sup>n</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_7.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 7:23</a>. <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_5.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 5:4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_4.15-16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 4:15-16</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Pet_3.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Pet 3:18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_3.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 3:18</a>. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_7.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 7:1</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp14"></a></p><h2>Chapter 14 –&nbsp;Of Saving Faith</h2><p>1. The grace&nbsp;of faith, whereby the elect are enabled to believe to the saving of their souls,<sup>a</sup>&nbsp;is the work of the Spirit of Christ in their hearts;<sup>b</sup> and is ordinarily wrought by the ministry of the Word:<sup>c</sup> by which also, and by the administration of the sacraments, and prayer, it is increased and strengthened.<sup>d</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.39" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 10:39</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_4.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 4:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.17-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:17-19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:8</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_10.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 10:14</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_10.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">17</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_2.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 2:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_20.32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 20:32</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_17.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 17:5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_1.16-17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 1:16-17</a>.</p><p>2. By this faith, a Christian believeth to be true whatsoever is revealed in the Word, for the authority of God Himself speaking therein;<sup>e</sup> and acteth differently upon that which each particular passage thereof containeth; yielding obedience to the commands,<sup>f</sup> trembling at the threatenings,<sup>g</sup> and embracing the promises of God for this life, and that which is to come.<sup>h</sup> But the principal acts of saving faith are accepting, receiving, and resting upon Christ alone for justification, sanctification, and eternal life, by virtue of the covenant of grace.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_4.42" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 4:42</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Thess_2.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Thess 2:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_5.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 5:10</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_24.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 24:14</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_16.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 16:26</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_66.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 66:2</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_11.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 11:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_4.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 4:8</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_1.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 1:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_16.31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 16:31</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_2.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 2:20</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_15.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 15:11</a>.</p><p>3. This faith is different in degrees, weak or strong;<sup>k</sup> may be often and many ways assailed, and weakened, but gets the victory;<sup>l</sup> &nbsp;growing up in many to the attainment of a full assurance through Christ,<sup>m</sup> who is both the author and finisher of our faith.<sup>n</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_5.13-14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 5:13-14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.19-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:19-20</a>;&nbsp;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_6.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 6:30</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_8.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt&nbsp;8:10</a>.&nbsp;<sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_22.31-32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 22:31-32</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_6.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 6:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1John_5.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1John 5:4-5</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_6.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 6:11-12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 10:22</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:2</a>. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_12.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 12:2</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp15"></a></p><h2>Chapter 15 –&nbsp;Of Repentance Unto Life</h2><p>1. Repentance unto life is an evangelical grace,<sup>a</sup> the doctrine whereof is to be preached by every minister of the gospel, as well as that of faith in Christ.<sup>b</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Zech_12.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Zech 12:10</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_11.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 11:18</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_24.47" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 24:47</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_1.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 1:15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_20.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 20:21</a>.</p><p>2. By it, a sinner, out of the sight and sense not only of the danger, but also of the filthiness and odiousness of his sins, as contrary to the holy nature and righteous law of God; and upon the apprehension of His mercy in Christ to such as are penitent, so grieves for, and hates his sins, as to turn from them all unto God,<sup>c</sup> purposing and endeavouring to walk with Him in all the ways of His commandments.<sup>d</sup></p><p><sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_18.30-31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 18:30-31</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_36.31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 36:31</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_30.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 30:22</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_51.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 51:4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Jer_31.18-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jer 31:18-19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Joel_2.12-13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Joel 2:12-13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Amos_5.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Amos 5:15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_119.128" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 119:128</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_7.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 7:11</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_119.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 119:6</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_119.59" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">59</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_119.106" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">106</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_1.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 1:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Kings_23.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Kings 23:25</a>.</p><p>3. Although repentance be not to be rested in, as any satisfaction for sin, or any cause of the pardon thereof,<sup>e</sup> which is the act of God’s free grace in Christ;<sup>f</sup> yet is it of such necessity to all sinners, that none may expect pardon without it.<sup>g</sup></p><p><sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_36.31-32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 36:31-32</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_16.61-63" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 16:61-63</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Hos_14.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Hos 14:2</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Hos_14.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_3.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 3:24</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:7</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_13.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 13:3</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_13.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_17.30-31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 17:30-31</a>.</p><p>4. As there is no sin so small, but it deserves damnation,<sup>h</sup> so there is no sin so great, that it can bring damnation upon those who truly repent.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_5.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 5:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_12.36" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 12:36</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_55.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 55:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_8.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 8:1</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_1.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 1:16</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_1.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">18</a>.</p><p>5. Men ought not to content themselves with a general repentance, but it is every man’s duty to endeavour to repent of his particular sins, particularly.<sup>k</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_19.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 19:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_19.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 19:8</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_1.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 1:13</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_1.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">15</a>.</p><p>6. As every man is bound to make private confession of his sins to God, praying for the pardon thereof;<sup>l</sup> upon which, and the forsaking of them, he shall find mercy:<sup>m</sup> so, he that scandalizeth his brother, or the Church of Christ, ought to be willing, by a private or public confession, and sorrow for his sin, to declare his repentance to those that are offended,<sup>n</sup> who are thereupon to be reconciled to him, and in love to receive him.<sup>o</sup></p><p><sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_51.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 51:4-5</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_51.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_51.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">7</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_51.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">9</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_51.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_32.5-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 32:5-6</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Prov_28.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Prov 28:13</a>; 1&nbsp;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_1.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 1:9</a>. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=James_5.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">James 5:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_17.3-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 17:3-4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Josh_7.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Josh 7:19</a>; Ps 51. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_2.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 2:8</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp16"></a></p><h2>Chapter 16 –&nbsp;Of Good Works</h2><p>1.
