<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1Cor_11.23-29" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1Cor 11:23-29</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.42" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:42</a>. <sup>x</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_6.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 6:13</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Neh_10.29" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Neh 10:29</a>. <sup>y</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_19.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 19:21</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eccl_5.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eccl 5:4-5</a>. <sup>z</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Joel_2.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Joel 2:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Esth_4.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Esth 4:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_9.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 9:15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 7:5</a>. <sup>a</sup>Ps 107; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Esth_9.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Esth 9:22</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_12.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 12:28</a>.</p><p>6. Neither prayer, nor any other part of religious worship, is now under the gospel either tied unto, or made more acceptable by any place in which it is performed, or towards which it is directed:<sup>c</sup> but God is to be worshipped everywhere,<sup>d</sup> in spirit and truth;<sup>e</sup> as in private families<sup>f</sup> daily,<sup>g</sup> and in secret each one by himself;<sup>h</sup> so, more solemnly, in the public assemblies, which are not carelessly or wilfully to be neglected, or forsaken, when God, by His Word or providence, calleth thereunto.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_4.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 4:21</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mal_1.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mal 1:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_2.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 2:8</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_4.23-24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 4:23-24</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Jer_10.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jer 10:25</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_6.6-7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 6:6-7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Job_1.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Job 1:5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Sam_6.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Sam 6:18</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Sam_6.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">20</a>;</p><p><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_3.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 3:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 10:2</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_6.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 6:11</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_6.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 6:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_6.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 6:18</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_56.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 56:6</a>, <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_56.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 10:25</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Prov_1.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Prov 1:20</a>, <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Prov_1.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">21</a>, <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Prov_1.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">24</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Prov_8.34" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Prov 8:34</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_13.42" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 13:42</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_4.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 4:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.42" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:42</a>.</p><p>7. As it is the law of nature, that, in general, a due proportion of time be set apart for the worship of God; so, in His Word, by a positive, moral, and perpetual commandment, binding all men, in all ages, He hath particularly appointed one day in seven, for a Sabbath, to be kept holy unto Him:<sup>k</sup> which, from the beginning of the world to the resurrection of Christ, was the last day of the week; and, from the resurrection of Christ, was changed into the first day of the week,<sup>l</sup> which, in Scripture, is called the Lord’s Day,<sup>m</sup> and is to be continued to the end of the world, as the Christian Sabbath.<sup>n</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_20.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 20:8</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_20.10-11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">10-11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_56.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 56:2</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_56.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">4</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_56.6-7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">6-7</a>. <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_2.2-3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 2:2-3</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_2.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_16.1-2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 16:1-2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_20.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 20:7</a>. <sup>m</sup> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_1.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rev 1:10</a>. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_20.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 20:8</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_20.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">10</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_5.17-18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 5:17-18</a>.</p><p>8. This Sabbath is then kept holy unto the Lord, when men, after a due preparing of their hearts, and ordering of their common affairs beforehand, do not only observe an holy rest, all the day, from their own works, words, and thoughts about their worldly employments, and recreations,<sup>o</sup> but also are taken up the whole time in the public and private exercises of His worship, and in the duties of necessity and mercy.<sup>p</sup></p><p><sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_20.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 20:8</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_16.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 16:23</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_16.25-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">25-26</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_16.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_16.29-30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">29-30</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_31.15-17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 31:15-17</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_58.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 58:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Neh_13.15-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Neh 13:15-19</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Neh_13.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Neh_13.21-22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">21-22</a>. <sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_58.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 58:13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_12.1-13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 12:1-13</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp22"></a></p><h2>Chapter 22 –&nbsp;Of Lawful Oaths and Vows</h2><p>1. A lawful oath is a part of religious worship,<sup>a</sup> wherein, upon just occasion, the person swearing solemnly calleth God to witness what he asserteth, or promiseth; and to judge him according to the truth or falsehood of what he sweareth.<sup>b</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_10.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 10:20</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_20.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 20:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Lev_19.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Lev 19:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_1.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 1:23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Chron_6.22-23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Chron 6:22-23</a>.</p><p>2. The name of God only is that by which men ought to swear; and therein it is to be used with all holy fear and reverence.<sup>c</sup> Therefore, to swear vainly or rashly, by that glorious and dreadful Name; or, to swear at all by any other thing, is sinful, and to be abhorred. <sup>d</sup>Yet, as in matters of weight and moment, an oath is warranted by the Word of God, under the New Testament, as well as under the Old;<sup>e</sup> so a lawful oath, being imposed by lawful authority, in such matters ought to be taken.<sup>f</sup></p><p><sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_6.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 6:13</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_20.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod&nbsp;20:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Jer_5.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jer 5:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_5.34" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 5:34</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_5.37" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">37</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=James_5.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">James&nbsp;5:12</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_6.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 6:16</a>;&nbsp;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_1.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor&nbsp;1:23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_65.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 65:16</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Kings_8.31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Kings 8:31</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Neh_13.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Neh 13:25</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezra_10.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezra 10:5</a>.</p><p>3. Whosoever taketh an oath ought duly to consider the weightiness of so solemn an act; and therein to avouch nothing, but what he is fully persuaded is the truth.<sup>g</sup> Neither may any man bind himself by oath to anything but what is good and just, and what he believeth so to be, and what he is able and resolved to perform.<sup>h</sup> Yet is it a sin to refuse an oath touching anything that is good and just, being imposed by lawful authority.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_20.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 20:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Jer_4.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jer 4:2</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_24.2-3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 24:2-3</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_24.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_24.5-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">5-6</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_24.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_24.8-9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">8-9</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Numb_5.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Numb 5:19</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Numb_5.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">21</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Neh_5.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Neh 5:12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_22.7-11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 22:7-11</a>.</p><p>4. An oath is to be taken in the plain and common sense of the words, without equivocation, or mental reservation.<sup>k</sup> It cannot oblige to sin: but in anything not sinful, being taken, it binds to performance, although to a man’s own hurt.<sup>l</sup> Nor is it to be violated, although made&nbsp;to&nbsp;heretics, or infidels.<sup>m</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Jer_4.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jer 4:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_24.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 24:4</a>; <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Sam_25.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Sam 25:22</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Sam_25.32-34" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">32-34</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_15.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 15:4</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_17.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 17:16</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_17.18-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">18-19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Josh_9.18-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Josh 9:18-19</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Sam_21.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Sam 21:1</a>.</p><p>5. A vow is of the like nature with a promissory oath, and ought to be made with the like religious care, and to be performed with the like faithfulness.<sup>n</sup></p><p><sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_19.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 19:21</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eccl_5.4-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eccl 5:4-6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_61.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 61:8</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_66.13-14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 66:13-14</a>.</p><p>6. It is not to be made to any creature, but to God alone:<sup>o</sup> and, that it may be accepted, it is to be made voluntarily, out of faith, and conscience of duty, in way of thankfulness for mercy received, or for the obtaining of what we want; whereby we more strictly bind ourselves to necessary duties; or to other things, so far and so long as they may fitly conduce thereunto.<sup>p</sup></p><p><sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_76.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 76:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Jer_44.25-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jer 44:25-26</a>. <sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_23.21-23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 23:21-23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_50.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps&nbsp;50:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_28.20-22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 28:20-22</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_28.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> 1&nbsp;Sam 1:11; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_66.13-14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 66:13-14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_132.2-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 132:2-5</a>.</p><p>7. No man may vow to do anything forbidden in the Word of God, or what would hinder any duty therein commanded, or which is not in his own power, and for the performance whereof he hath no promise of ability from God.<sup>q</sup> In which respects, Popish monastical vows of perpetual single life, professed poverty, and regular obedience, are so far from being degrees of higher perfection, that they are superstitious and sinful snares, in which no Christian may entangle himself.<sup>r</sup></p><p><sup>q</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_23.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 23:12</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_23.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_6.26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 6:26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Numb_30.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Numb 30:5</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Numb_30.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">8</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Numb_30.12-13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">12-13</a>. <sup>r</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_19.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 19:11-12</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_19.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 7:2</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_4.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 4:28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_4.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 4:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 7:23</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp23"></a></p><h2>Chapter 23 –&nbsp;Of the Civil Magistrate</h2><p>1. God, the supreme Lord and King of all the world, hath ordained civil magistrates, to be, under Him, over the people, for His own glory, and the public good: and, to this end, hath armed them with the power of the sword, for the defence and encouragement of them that are good, and for the punishment of evil doers.<sup>a</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_13.1-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 13:1-4</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_13.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_2.13-14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 2:13-14</a>.</p><p>2. It is lawful for Christians to accept and execute the office of a magistrate, when called thereunto;<sup>b</sup> in the managing whereof, as they ought especially to maintain piety, justice, and peace, according to the wholesome laws of each commonwealth;<sup>c</sup> so for that end, they may lawfully now, under the New Testament, wage war, upon just and necessary occasion.<sup>d</sup></p><p><sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Prov_8.15-16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Prov 8:15-16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_13.1-2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 13:1-2</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_13.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_13.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">4</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_2.10-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 2:10-12</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_2.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_2.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 2:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_82.3-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 82:3-4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Sam_23.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Sam 23:3</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_2.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 2:13</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_3.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 3:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_13.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 13:4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_8.9-10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 8:9-10</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.1-2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 10:1-2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_17.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rev 17:14</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_17.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">16</a>.</p><p>3. The civil magistrate may not assume to himself the administration of the Word and sacraments, or the power of the keys of the kingdom of heaven:<sup>e</sup> yet he hath authority, and it is his duty, to take order, that unity and peace be preserved in the Church, that the truth of God be kept pure and entire; that all blasphemies and heresies be suppressed; all corruptions and abuses in worship and discipline prevented or reformed; and all the ordinances of God duly settled, administered, and observed.<sup>f</sup> For the better effecting whereof, he hath power to call synods, to be present at them, and to provide that whatsoever is transacted in them be according to the mind of God.<sup>g</sup></p><p><sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Chron_26.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Chron 26:18</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_18.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 18:17</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_16.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 16:19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_12.28-29" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 12:28-29</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_4.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 4:11-12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_4.1-2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 4:1-2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_10.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 10:15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_5.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 5:4</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_4.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 4 9</a>:23; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_122.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 122:9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezra_7.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezra 7:23</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezra_7.25-28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">25-28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Lev_24.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Lev 24:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_13.5-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 13:5-6</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_13.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_13.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Kings_18.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Kings 18:4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Chron_13.1-9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Chron 13:1-9</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Chron_13.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Kings_23.1-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Kings 23:1-26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Chron_34.33" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Chron 34:33</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Chron_15.12-13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Chron 15:12-13</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Chron_19.8-11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Chron 19:8-11</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Chron_19.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> 2 Chron 29-30; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_2.4-5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 2:4-5</a>.</p><p>4. It is the duty of people to pray for magistrates,<sup>h</sup> to honour their persons,<sup>i</sup> to pay them tribute and other dues,<sup>k</sup> to obey their lawful commands, and to be subject to their authority, for conscience’ sake.<sup>l</sup> Infidelity, or difference in religion, doth not make void the magistrates’ just and legal authority, nor free the people from their due obedience to them:<sup>m</sup> from which ecclesiastical persons are not exempted;<sup>n</sup> much less hath the Pope any power and jurisdiction over them in their dominions, or over any of their people; and, least of all, to deprive them of their dominions, or lives, if he shall judge them to be heretics, or upon any other pretence whatsoever.<sup>o</sup></p><p><sup>h</sup>1 &nbsp;Tim 2:1-2. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_2.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 2:17</a>. <sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_13.6-7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 13:6-7</a>. <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_13.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 13:5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tit 3:1</a>.&nbsp;<sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_2.13-14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 2:13-14</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_2.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_2.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">16</a>. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_13.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 13:1</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Kings_2.35" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Kings 2:35</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_25.9-11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 25:9-11</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_25.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Pet_2.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Pet 2:1</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Pet_2.10-11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">10-11</a>; Jude 8-11. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Thess_2.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Thess 2:4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_13.15-17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rev 13:15-17</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp24"></a></p><h2>Chapter 24 –&nbsp;Of Marriage and Divorce</h2><p>1. Marriage is to be between one man and one woman: neither is it lawful for any man to have more than one wife, nor for any woman to have more than one husband; at the same time.<sup>a</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_2.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 2:24</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_19.5-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 19:5-6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Prov_2.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Prov 2:17</a>.</p><p>2. Marriage was ordained for the mutual help of husband and wife,<sup>b</sup> for the increase of mankind with a legitimate issue, and of the Church with an holy seed;<sup>c</sup> and for preventing of uncleanness.<sup>d</sup></p><p><sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_2.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 2:18</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mal_2.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mal 2:15</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 7:2</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">9</a>.</p><p>3. It is lawful for all sorts of people to marry, who are able with judgment to give their consent.<sup>e</sup> Yet it is the duty of Christians to marry only in the Lord:<sup>f</sup> and therefore such as profess the true reformed religion should not marry with infidels, papists, or other idolaters: neither should such as are godly be unequally yoked, by marrying with such as are notoriously wicked in their life, or maintain damnable heresies.<sup>g</sup></p><p><sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_13.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 13:4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_4.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 4:3</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.36-38" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 7:36-38</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_24.57-58" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 24:57-58</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.39" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 7:39</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_34.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 34:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_34.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 34:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_7.3-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 7:3-4</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_7.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Kings_11.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Kings 11:4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Neh_13.25-27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Neh 13:25-27</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mal_2.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mal 2:11-12</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mal_2.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_6.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 6:14</a>.</p><p>4. Marriage ought not to be within the degrees of consanguinity or affinity forbidden in the Word;<sup>h</sup> nor can such incestuous marriages ever be made lawful by any law of man or consent of parties, so as those persons may live together as man and wife.<sup>i</sup> The man may not marry any of his wife’s kindred nearer in blood than he may of his own; nor the woman of her husband’s kindred nearer in blood than of her own.<sup>k</sup></p><p><sup>h</sup>Lev 18; 1 Cor 5:1; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Amos_2.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Amos 2:7</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_6.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 6:18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Lev_18.24-28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Lev 18:24-28</a>. <sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Lev_20.19-21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Lev 20:19-21</a>.</p><p>5. Adultery or fornication committed after a contract, being detected before marriage, giveth just occasion to the innocent party to dissolve that contract.<sup>l</sup> In the case of adultery after marriage, it is lawful for the innocent party to sue out a divorce:<sup>m</sup> and, after the divorce, to marry another, as if the offending party were dead.<sup>n</sup></p><p><sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_1.18-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 1:18-20</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_5.31-32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 5:31-32</a>. <sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_19.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 19:9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_7.2-3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 7:2-3</a>.</p><p>6. Although the corruption of man be such as is apt to study arguments unduly to put asunder those whom God hath joined together in marriage: yet nothing but adultery, or such wilful desertion as can no way be remedied by the Church or civil magistrate, is cause sufficient of dissolving the bond of marriage:<sup>o</sup> wherein, a public and orderly course of proceeding is to be observed; and the persons concerned in it not left to their own wills and discretion, in their own case.<sup>p</sup></p><p><sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_19.8-9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 19:8-9</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_19.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 7:15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_19.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 19:6</a>. <sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Deut_24.1-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Deut 24:1-4</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp25"></a></p><h2>Chapter 25 –&nbsp;Of the Church</h2><p>1. The catholic or universal Church which is invisible, consists of the whole number of the elect, that have been, are, or shall be gathered into one, under Christ the Head thereof; and is the spouse, the body, the fulness of Him that filleth all in all.<sup>a</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:10</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.22-23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">22-23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_5.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 5:23</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_5.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">27</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_5.32" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">32</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_1.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 1:18</a>.</p><p>2. The visible Church, which is also catholic or universal under the gospel (not confined to one nation as before under the law), consists of all those throughout the world that profess the true religion;<sup>b</sup> and of their children:<sup>c</sup> and is the kingdom of the Lord Jesus Christ,<sup>d</sup> the house and family of God,<sup>e</sup> out of which there is no ordinary possibility of salvation.<sup>f</sup></p><p><sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_1.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 1:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_12.12-13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 12:12-13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_2.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 2:8</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_7.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rev 7:9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_15.9-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 15:9-12</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 7:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.39" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:39</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_16.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ezek 16:20</a>, <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ezek_16.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">21</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_11.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 11:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_3.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 3:15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_17.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 17:7</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_13.47" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 13:47</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_9.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 9:7</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_3.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 3:15</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.47" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:47</a>.</p><p>3. Unto this catholic visible Church Christ hath given the ministry, oracles, and ordinances of God, for the gathering and perfecting of the saints, in this life, to the end of the world: and doth by His own presence and Spirit, according to His promise, make them effectual thereunto.<sup>g</sup></p><p><sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_12.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 12:28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_4.11-13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 4:11-13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19</a>, <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">20</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_59.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 59:21</a>.</p><p>4. This catholic Church hath been sometimes more, sometimes less visible.<sup>h</sup> And particular Churches, which are members thereof, are more or less pure, according as the doctrine of the gospel is taught and embraced, ordinances administered, and public worship performed more or less purely in them.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_11.3-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 11:3-4</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_12.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rev 12:6</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_12.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>. <sup>i</sup>Rev 2-3; 1 Cor 5:6-7.</p><p>5. The purest Churches under heaven are subject both to mixture and error:<sup>k</sup> and some have so degenerated, as to become no Churches of Christ, but synagogues of Satan.<sup>l</sup> Nevertheless, there shall be always a Church on earth, to worship God according to His will.<sup>m</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_13.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 13:12</a>; Rev 2-3; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_13.24-30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 13:24-30</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_13.24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_13.47" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">47</a>. <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_18.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rev 18:2</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_11.18-22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 11:18-22</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_16.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 16:18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_72.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 72:17</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_102.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 102:28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19-20</a>.</p><p>6. There is no other head of the Church, but the Lord Jesus Christ;<sup>n</sup> nor can the Pope of Rome, in any sense, be head thereof; but is that Antichrist, that man of sin, and son of perdition, that exalteth himself, in the Church, against Christ and all that is called God.<sup>o</sup></p><p><sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_1.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 1:18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_1.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 1:22</a>. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_23.8-10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 23:8-10</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_23.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Thess_2.3-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Thess 2:3-4</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Thess_2.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Thess_2.8-9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">8-9</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rev_13.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rev 13:6</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp26"></a></p><h2>Chapter 26 –&nbsp;Of the Communion of Saints</h2><p>1. All saints, that are united to Jesus Christ their&nbsp;Head by His Spirit&nbsp;and by faith, have fellowship with Him in His graces, sufferings, death, resurrection, and glory:<sup>a</sup> and, being united to one another in love, they have communion in each other’s gifts and graces,<sup>b</sup> and are obliged to the performance of such duties, public and private, as do conduce to their mutual good, both in the inward and outward man.<sup>c</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_1.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 1:3</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_3.16-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 3:16-19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_1.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 1:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_2.5-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 2:5-6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Phil_3.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Phil 3:10</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.5-6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:5-6</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Tim_2.12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Tim 2:12</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_4.15-16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 4:15-16</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_4.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_12.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 12:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_3.21-23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 3:21-23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:19</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Thess_5.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Thess 5:11</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Thess_5.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_1.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 1:11-12</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_1.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_1.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_3.16-18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 3:16-18</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_6.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 6:10</a>.</p><p>2. Saints by profession are bound to maintain a holy fellowship and communion in the worship of God; and in performing such other spiritual services as tend to their mutual edification;<sup>d</sup> as also in relieving each other in outward things, according to their several abilities, and necessities. Which communion, as God offereth opportunity, is to be extended unto all those who, in every place, call upon the name of the Lord Jesus.<sup>e</sup></p><p><sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.24-25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 10:24-25</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.42" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:42</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.46" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">46</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_2.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 2:3</a>; 1&nbsp;Cor 11:20. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.44-45" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:44-45</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.44" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20John_3.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 John 3:17</a>; 2 Cor 8-9; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_11.29-30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 11:29-30</a>.</p><p>3. This communion, which the saints have with Christ, doth not make them, in any wise, partakers of the substance of His Godhead; or to be equal with Christ, in any respect: either of which to affirm is impious and blasphemous.<sup>f</sup> Nor doth their communion one with another, as saints, take away, or infringe the title or property which each man hath in his goods and possessions.<sup>g</sup></p><p><sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_1.18-19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 1:18-19</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_1.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_8.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 8:6</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Isa_42.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Isa 42:8</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Tim_6.15-16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Tim 6:15-16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Ps_45.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ps 45:7</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_1.8-9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 1:8-9</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_20.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 20:15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_4.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 4:28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_5.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 5:4</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp27"></a></p><h2>Chapter 27 –&nbsp;Of the Sacraments</h2><p>1. Sacraments are holy signs and seals of the covenant of grace,<sup>a</sup> immediately instituted by God,&lt;supb to represent Christ and His benefits; and to confirm our interest in Him;<sup>c</sup> as also, to put a visible difference between those that belong unto the Church, and the rest of the world;<sup>d</sup> and solemnly to engage them to the service of God in Christ, according to His Word.<sup>e</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_17.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 17:7</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_17.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">10</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:23</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_10.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 10:16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.25-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:25-26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 3:17</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_15.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 15:8</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_12.48" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 12:48</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_34.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 34:14</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.3-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:3-4</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.3" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_10.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 10:16</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_10.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">21</a>.</p><p>2. There is in every sacrament a spiritual relation, or sacramental union, between the sign and the thing signified: whence it comes to pass, that the names and effects of the one are attributed to the other.<sup>f</sup></p><p><sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_17.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 17:10</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_26.27-28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 26:27-28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tit 3:5</a>.</p><p>3. The grace which is exhibited in or by the sacraments rightly used, is not conferred by any power in them: neither doth the efficacy of a sacrament depend upon the piety or intention of him that doth administer it:<sup>g</sup> but upon the work of the Spirit,<sup>h</sup> and the word of institution, which contains, together with a precept authorizing the use thereof, a promise of benefit to worthy receivers.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_2.28-29" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 2:28-29</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_2.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Pet_3.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Pet 3:21</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_3.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 3:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_12.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 12:13</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_26.27-28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 26:27-28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19-20</a>.</p><p>4. There be only two sacraments ordained by Christ our Lord in the gospel; that is to say, Baptism and the Supper of the Lord: neither of which may be dispensed by any but by a minister of the Word lawfully ordained.<sup>k</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:20</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_4.1" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 4:1</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_5.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 5:4</a>.</p><p>5. The sacraments of the Old Testament, in regard of the spiritual things thereby signified and exhibited, were, for substance, the same with those of the New.<sup>l</sup></p><p><sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_10.1-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 10:1-4</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp28"></a></p><h2>Chapter 28 –&nbsp;Of Baptism</h2><p>1. Baptism is a sacrament of the New Testament, ordained by Jesus Christ,<sup>a</sup> not only for the solemn admission of the party baptized into the visible Church;<sup>b</sup> but also, to be unto him a sign and seal of the covenant of grace,<sup>c</sup> of his ingrafting into Christ,<sup>d</sup> of regeneration,<sup>e</sup> of remission of sins,<sup>f</sup> and of his giving up unto God through Jesus Christ, to walk in newness of life.<sup>g</sup> Which sacrament is, by Christ’s own appointment, to be continued in His Church until the end of the world.<sup>h</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19</a>. <sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_12.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 12:13</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:11</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:11-12</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 3:27</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:5</a>. <sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tit 3:5</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_1.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 1:4</a>. <sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_6.3-4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 6:3-4</a>. <sup>h</sup> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19-20</a>.</p><p>2. The outward element to be used in this sacrament is water, wherewith the party is to be baptized, in the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Ghost, by a minister of the gospel, lawfully called thereunto.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_3.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 3:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_1.33" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 1:33</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19-20</a>.</p><p>3. Dipping of the person into the water is not necessary: but baptism is rightly administered by pouring or sprinkling water upon the person.<sup>k</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 9:10</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.19-22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">19-22</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.41" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:41</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_16.33" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 16:33</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_7.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 7:4</a>.</p><p>4. Not only those that do actually profess faith in and obedience unto Christ,<sup>l</sup> but also the infants of one or both believing parents, are to be baptized.<sup>m</sup></p><p><sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_16.15-16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 16:15-16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_8.37-38" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 8:37-38</a>. <sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_17.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gen 17:7</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gen_17.9-10" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">9-10</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 3:9</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Col_2.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Col 2:11-12</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.38-39" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:38-39</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:11-12</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_7.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 7:14</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_28.19" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 28:19</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_10.13-16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 10:13-16</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_18.15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 18:15</a>.</p><p>5. Although it be a great sin to contemn or neglect this ordinance,<sup>n</sup> yet grace and salvation are not so inseparably annexed unto it, as that no person can be regenerated or saved without it;<sup>o</sup> or, that all that are baptized are undoubtedly regenerated.<sup>p</sup></p><p><sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_7.30" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 7:30</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Exod_4.24-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exod 4:24-26</a>. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Rom_4.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rom 4:11</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.2" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 10:2</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.4" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">4</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">22</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.31" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">31</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.45" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">45</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_10.47" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">47</a>. <sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_8.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 8:13</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_8.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">23</a>.</p><p>6. The efficacy of baptism is not tied to that moment of time wherein it is administered;<sup>q</sup> yet notwithstanding, by the right use of this ordinance, the grace promised is not only offered, but really exhibited and conferred, by the Holy Ghost, to such (whether of age or infants) as that grace belongeth unto, according to the counsel of God’s own will, in His appointed time.<sup>r</sup></p><p><sup>q</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_3.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">John 3:5</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=John_3.8" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">8</a>. <sup>r</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Gal_3.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Gal 3:27</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tit 3:5</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Eph_5.25-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Eph 5:25-26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.38" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 2:38</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_2.41" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">41</a>.</p><p>7. The sacrament of baptism is but once to be administered unto any person.<sup>s</sup></p><p><sup>s</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Tit_3.5" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tit 3:5</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp29"></a></p><h2>Chapter 29 –&nbsp;Of the Lord’s Supper</h2><p>1. Our Lord Jesus, in the night wherein He was betrayed, instituted the sacrament of His body and blood, called the Lord’s Supper, to be observed in His Church, unto the end of the world, for the perpetual remembrance of the sacrifice of Himself in His death; the sealing all benefits thereof unto true believers, their spiritual nourishment and growth in Him, their further engagement in and to all duties which they owe unto Him; and to be a bond and pledge of their communion with Him, and with each other, as members of His mystical body.<sup>a</sup></p><p><sup>a</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.23-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:23-26</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_10.16-17" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 10:16-17</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_10.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_10.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">21</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_12.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 12:13</a>.</p><p>2. In this sacrament, Christ is not offered up to His Father; nor any real sacrifice made at all for remission of sins of the quick or dead;<sup>b</sup> but only a commemoration of that one offering up of Himself, by Himself, upon the cross, once for all: and a spiritual oblation of all possible praise unto God for the same:<sup>c</sup> so that the Popish sacrifice of the mass (as they call it) is most abominably injurious to Christ’s one, only sacrifice, the alone propitiation for all the sins of His elect.<sup>d</sup></p><p><sup>b</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.22" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 9:22</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.25-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">25-26</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.25" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_9.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">28</a>. <sup>c</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.24-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:24-26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_26.26-27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 26:26-27</a>. <sup>d</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_7.23-24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 7:23-24</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_7.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_7.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">27</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.11-12" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Heb 10:11-12</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.11" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.14" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Heb_10.18" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">18</a>.</p><p>3. The Lord Jesus hath, in this ordinance, appointed His ministers to declare His word of institution to the people; to pray, and bless the elements of bread and wine, and thereby to set them apart from a common to a holy use; and to take and break the bread, to take the cup, and (they communicating also themselves) to give both to the communicants;<sup>e</sup> but to none who are not then present in the congregation.<sup>f</sup></p><p><sup>e</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_26.26-28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 26:26-28</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_14.22-24" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 14:22-24</a> and <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_22.19-20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 22:19-20</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.23-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:23-26</a>. <sup>f</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_20.7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 20:7</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.20" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:20</a>.</p><p>4. Private masses, or receiving this sacrament by a priest or any other alone;<sup>g</sup> as likewise, the denial of the cup to the people,<sup>h</sup> worshipping the elements, the lifting them up or carrying them about for adoration, and the reserving them for any pretended religious use; are all contrary to the nature of this sacrament, and to the institution of Christ.<sup>i</sup></p><p><sup>g</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_10.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 10:16</a>. <sup>h</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Mark_14.23" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mark 14:23</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.25-29" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:25-29</a>. <sup>i</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_15.9" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 15:9</a>.</p><p>5. The outward elements in this sacrament, duly set apart to the uses ordained by Christ, have such relation to Him crucified, as that, truly, yet sacramentally only, they are sometimes called by the name of the things they represent, to wit, the body and blood of Christ;<sup>k</sup> albeit in substance and nature they still remain truly and only bread and wine, as they were before.<sup>l</sup></p><p><sup>k</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_26.26-28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 26:26-28</a>. <sup>l</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.26-28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:26-28</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_26.29" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 26:29</a>.</p><p>6. That doctrine which maintains a change of the substance of bread and wine into the substance of Christ’s body and blood (commonly called transubstantiation) by consecration of a priest, or by any other way, is repugnant, not to Scripture alone, but even to common sense and reason; overthroweth the nature of the sacrament, and hath been, and is the cause of manifold superstitions; yea, of gross idolatries.<sup>m</sup></p><p><sup>m</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Acts_3.21" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Acts 3:21</a> with <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.24-26" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:24-26</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_24.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Luke 24:6</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Luke_24.39" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">39</a>.</p><p>7. Worthy receivers outwardly partaking of the visible elements in this sacrament,<sup>n</sup> do then also, inwardly by faith, really and indeed, yet not carnally and corporally, but spiritually, receive and feed upon Christ crucified, and all benefits of His death: the body and blood of Christ being then, not corporally or carnally, in, with, or under the bread and wine; yet, as really, but spiritually, present to the faith of believers in that ordinance, as the elements themselves are to their outward senses.<sup>o</sup></p><p><sup>n</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.28" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:28</a>. <sup>o</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_10.16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 10:16</a>.</p><p>8. Although ignorant and wicked men receive the outward elements in this sacrament: yet they receive not the thing signified thereby, but by their unworthy coming thereunto are guilty of the body and blood of the Lord to their own damnation. Wherefore, all ignorant and ungodly persons, as they are unfit to enjoy communion with Him, so are they unworthy of the Lord’s table; and cannot, without great sin against Christ while they remain such, partake of these holy mysteries,<sup>p</sup> or be admitted thereunto.<sup>q</sup></p><p><sup>p</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.27-29" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 11:27-29</a>;<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_11.27" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a> <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Cor_6.14-16" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Cor 6:14-16</a>. <sup>q</sup><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_5.6-7" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1 Cor 5:6-7</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_5.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener"></a><a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=1%20Cor_5.13" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">13</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Thess_3.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2 Thess 3:6</a>,<a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=2%20Thess_3.14-15" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14-15</a>; <a href="https://av1611.com/verseclick/gobible.php?p=Matt_7.6" class="vcVerseLink" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Matt 7:6</a>.</p><p><a href="#index">Return to Chapter Index</a></p><hr><p><a name="cp30"></a></p><h2>Chapter 30 –&nbsp;Of Church Censures</h2><p>1.
